# Bhagavad Gita — Image Generation Prompts

Each verse below has one self-contained image prompt. Square 1:1 composition. Cinematic Mahabharata-era Indian epic style, devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic lighting. Lord Krishna is always rendered as the strongest, mightiest, and most handsome warrior in every frame.

Surface and texture style (applies to every prompt): every surface in the image is simple, clean, and solid. Krishna's blue skin is one clean uniform deep blue color, completely smooth, like a single painted plane — no texture, no markings, no patterns, no highlights on the skin itself. All human skin in every figure is plain matte and even-toned. Silk cloth is a single solid color (yellow for Krishna, white for Arjuna, crimson for Bhima, etc.) with at most a thin plain border at the edge. Armor is solid metal in one color (silver, gold, bronze) with simple geometric shape and no surface carving. The chariot is solid gold with clean simple lines. The sky is open and clear. Faces are calm, dry, and smooth. Jewels appear only as discrete pieces on Krishna's crown, Arjuna's diadem, and Karna's earrings — and look like 2-3 large jewels, not many small ones.

Age & maturity rule (applies to every prompt): every warrior on screen is a mature adult man, never a teenager or boy. Default age is mid-thirties to mid-forties — broad-shouldered, battle-hardened, full grown body, with a beard or thick mustache. Even the youngest named warriors (Abhimanyu and the five Upapandavas / sons of Draupadi) are mature adult warriors in their late twenties — strong, fully grown, with short trim beards and weathered features — never beardless boys, never adolescents, never smooth-faced youths. No depiction may render any named warrior as a teenager.

## Chapter 1 - Arjuna Visada Yoga

### 1.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of the blind Kuru king Dhritarashtra seated in a dim Hastinapura royal chamber, draped in white-and-gold royal robes and turban, his cloudy sightless eyes turned slightly upward, long silver beard flowing across his broad chest, weary hands resting on the carved armrests of a teakwood throne. Beside him stands Sanjaya, mature and dignified, in saffron-cream robes with a sandalwood tilak on his forehead, palms joined as his far-seeing visionary eyes gaze into a distant golden vision of Kurukshetra battlefield where two vast armies face one another at dawn. Oil lamps flicker on bronze stands; tall pillars rise into shadow. The mood is heavy with foreboding, lit by warm amber lamplight and the cool blue dawn glow leaking through the high arches. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

### 1.2

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of King Duryodhana striding across the dusty plain of Kurukshetra toward his teacher Drona, his dark crimson-and-black armor edged in heavy gold, thick black mustache curled, fierce arrogant eyes narrowed, a heavy solid iron mace gripped in his right hand and his serpent-naga banner snapping overhead in the wind. Before him stands Drona, the brahmin-guru-warrior, elderly with a long white beard and ascetic face, saffron robes layered under smooth steel breastplate, holding his great longbow upright. Behind them, the vast Pandava army stretches into the distance, banners and elephants visible against the soft morning sky. Cool steel-grey light, pale dust kicked up by armored feet, war-banners fluttering. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. Beside him stands Drona, white-bearded and ascetic, listening with stern composure, longbow in hand. In the distance, Dhrishtadyumna, fire-born commander of the Pandava army, stands at the army's vanguard in copper-red flame-colored armor, his sharp piercing eyes lit by an inner flame, long sword and longbow ready. The horizon glows pale gold, soft warm air between the two camps. Mood of charged anticipation. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. ### 1.26

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Arjuna seen close, his face slowly transforming as recognition strikes him. ## Chapter 2 - Sankhya Yoga

### 2.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Arjuna sunk on the chariot floor, eyes brimming, breathing unsteady, his armor dusty, his bow lying beside him. Krishna, the supreme luminous presence, towers above him at the reins, deep sapphire-blue skin in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head and, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible across his sculpted chest, his beautifully chiseled handsome face bent gently downward toward his friend, lips parting to speak the first word of his teaching. The Hanuman banner ripples softly above. The two armies are softly blurred on either side. The light is a hush of gold-blue; the air is motionless in the moment of sacred beginning. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. ### 2.2

His beautifully serene magnetic face is touched with a gentle frown of concern. Arjuna, slumped on the chariot seat, looks up with tear-stained eyes, his Kiriti diadem catching a beam of late-morning sun. The Sudarshana Chakra spins quietly at Krishna's other hand. The light is warm and clarifying, the shadows soft. Mood: the first awakening. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. ## Chapter 3 - Karma Yoga

## Chapter 6 - Dhyana Yoga

### 6.1

Krishna, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, draws a clear visual contrast between true sannyasi and empty form. Arjuna observes with fresh understanding. Light is contrasting, clarifying. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. Krishna, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, illustrates that no one becomes a yogi who has not renounced thoughts. Arjuna observes the thought-gathering. Light is contemplative, clarifying. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. ## Chapter 7 - Gyaan Vigyana Yoga

### 7.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna leaning forward with both luminous magnificent hands extended in an opening invitation — hear how you shall fully know Me, with mind intent on Me, practising yoga and taking refuge in Me. Krishna, the supreme presence, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head with inner light, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible across his sculpted chest. ## Chapter 8 - Akshara Brahma Yoga

### 8.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Arjuna leaning forward to ask, his mighty handsome face bright with curiosity, his hands open in respectful inquiry. Krishna stands beside him at the reins, the supreme presence, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, listening warmly with an inviting smile, ready to receive the question. The Hanuman banner streams above. Light is questioning, expectant gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

### 8.2

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Arjuna asking earnestly: who is Adhiyajna here in this body, and how at the time of death may you be known by the self-controlled? Krishna stands beside him, the supreme luminous presence, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, listening with deep teaching attention. Light is contemplative, late afternoon. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

### 8.3

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna gesturing reverently to a vast translucent radiance labeled in soft visual gesture as the Imperishable brahman, the Supreme — Self-knowledge as a softly glowing inner light, and karma as a faint flame on a small altar by his feet. ## Chapter 9 - Raja Vidya Yoga

### 9.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna leaning intimately toward Arjuna, the supreme luminous presence, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible. Between them a translucent jewel-of-secrets pulses with profound knowledge — combined with experience. Krishna offers it openly, only to one who does not cavil. Arjuna's mighty handsome face is rapt with sacred attention. Light is intimate, jewel-bright. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

### 9.2

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna holding aloft a bright translucent crown — the kingly science, the kingly secret — golden and shining, dharma-aligned, easy to perform, eternal. Krishna, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, smiles softly: it is realisable by direct intuitional knowledge. Arjuna gazes at the radiant crown. Light is regal-radiant gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. Arjuna observes the warning. Light is fading-versus-radiant. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. ### 9.6

### 9.7

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of all beings — translucent figures of every kind — entering Krishna's prakriti at the end of a Kalpa, swirled gently into a soft luminous nest within him; and at the beginning of a new Kalpa, Krishna sending them forth again from his cosmic chest in fresh radiance. ## Chapter 10 - Vibhooti Yoga

### 10.1

Krishna's beautifully chiseled face shines with affectionate teaching. Arjuna sits at his feet, mighty handsome face lit with sacred attention. The Hanuman banner streams above the chariot. Light is renewed teaching gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. Arjuna observes the saints of the unmanifest path. Light is welfare-compassion gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

## Chapter 14 - Gunatraya Vibhaga Yoga

### 14.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna leaning forward with renewed teaching delight, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, beginning a higher knowledge — having known which all sages have gone to supreme perfection. A faint translucent line of past sages glows behind him, having reached perfection. Arjuna sits attentive. Light is higher-knowledge gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. Arjuna observes. Light is upward-clarity gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. ## Chapter 18 - spiritual freedom Sanyaas Yoga

### 18.1

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Arjuna leaning forward with deepest curiosity, mighty handsome face full of inquiry — I desire to know severally the truth of renunciation and abandonment, O Hrishikesha, slayer of Keshi. Krishna stands beside him at the reins, the supreme presence, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible, listening with infinite teaching warmth. Light is final-question gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light. No modern objects, no gore, no severed bodies, no caricature, no text or captions or watermarks or logos, no extra fingers. All surfaces are simple and clean: Krishna's blue skin is one uniform smooth color with no texture, all skin is plain and matte, silk cloth is solid color with at most a plain border, armor is solid metal in one color with simple shape, the air and sky are clear and uncluttered.

### 18.2

A square 1:1 cinematic Mahabharata-era painting of Krishna distinguishing two terms with two soft luminous gestures — sannyasa visualized as a translucent figure setting aside desire-driven karma; tyaga visualized as another translucent figure performing actions but releasing the fruits like petals into a breeze. Krishna, deep sapphire-blue body in one smooth uniform color, with a soft golden halo behind his head, peacock-feather crown bright, vaijayanti garland of forest flowers visible. Arjuna observes the careful distinction. Light is two-fold definition gold. Devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic light.
